@PAPER_ENTROPY
TITLE; Entropy is an Interface: Reversibility Below, Irreversibility at Commit
ONE_LINER; Entropy is recognition-relative code length; the second law lives at the readout channel, not in the substrate.

CLAIMS
C1; Substrate dynamics are exactly conservative (closed-loop flux=0); any "entropy production" is growth of codelength at the (W,K) interface.
C2; Maxwell's demon pays at commit: ŒîWork ‚â• k_B T ln 2 ¬∑ ŒîS_bits; reversible bulk steps do not alter S absent recognition commits.
C3; Changing the window/kernel (W,K) changes measured S in a law-governed way; aligned 8-tick windows preserve invariants (no spurious entropy).

FOUNDATIONS (math, minimal)
F1; Entropy as MDL @ channel: S_{W,K}(Œº) = L^*(p_Y), p_Y(y)=‚à´K(y|W(x)) dŒº(x). Special cases: (i) Shannon/Hartley when code optimal over Y; (ii) Gibbs when p_Y is Gibbsian.
F2; Monotonicity: For any post-processing Y‚ÜíZ via a stochastic map Q (data-processing), L^*(p_Z) ‚â• L^*(p_Y) up to O(1); hence entropy increases under further coarse-graining.
F3; Arrow-of-time = commit order: A recognition pipeline Œ† = (W_1,K_1)‚Üícommit‚Üí(W_2,K_2)‚Üícommit‚Ä¶ yields S_{Œ†} nondecreasing at each commit; bulk reversible steps with no commit keep S fixed.
F4; Landauer bridge: Reversible micro-evolution allows isothermal erasure cost bounded by k_B T ln 2 per bit of log-loss; identify ŒîS_bits with MDL code surplus removed at commit.
F5; Eight-tick alignment: Using PatternMeasurement lemmas, if windows respect 8-tick alignment, block sums equal Z(w) and observed averages equal the invariant; entropy does not grow from mere realignment.

CLASSICAL MAP
MAP; Boltzmann S = k_B ln Œ©; here Œ© counts instrument-distinguishable microstates under (W,K); if (W,K) refines, Œ© grows and S rises.
MAP; Shannon S = ‚àí‚àëp log p; exactly the MDL-optimal code length for readouts; our S reduces to Shannon when modeling Y directly.
MAP; Clausius; dQ_rev/T = dS at commit for quasistatic channels; identify "heat" with energy flushed by erasures/log-loss.

OPERATIONAL (no new experiments; archival-only demonstrations)
DATASETS
D1; Blackbody spectra (calibrated archives): show L(human: Planck law + few params + noise) ¬´ L(agnostic baselines) and derive S_{W,K} consistency across instruments.
D2; Gas expansion/compression textbook curves (archival labs): recompute S deltas as code deltas under declared (W,K); demonstrate independence from micro-path given same commits.
D3; Time series with reversible micro-models (simple Hamiltonian simulations from archives): show S fixed until a quantized commit (coarse binning / record) is applied.

DERIVATIONS (sketches to include in Methods)
DR1; DPI‚ÜíMonotone: prove S_{W,K} nondecrease along Œ† using code-length form of Kraft‚ÄìMcMillan + data-processing inequality.
DR2; Landauer bound: derive W_min ‚â• k_B T ln 2 ¬∑ ŒîS_bits from one-shot coding theorem + thermal reservoir arguments; note equality in quasistatic limit.
DR3; 8-tick invariants: use sumFirst8/blockSumAligned8 lemmas to prove zero alias entropy when windows are aligned; misalignment yields predictable code swell.

FALSIFIERS
F1; Find a repeatable pipeline where S decreases across a commit without exporting work/negentropy elsewhere.
F2; Show measured S independence from (W,K) choice in regimes where our theory predicts dependence (e.g., swap coarse bins but observe unchanged S beyond O(1)).
F3; Construct a demon whose full accounting (including its memory commits) undercuts the Landauer bound.

OUTPUT ARTIFACTS
FIG; Channel diagram with commits (bulk reversible vs commit steps).
FIG; Aligned vs misaligned 8-tick windows and entropy trajectories.
APP; Formal definition of S_{W,K} and proofs of DR1‚ÄìDR3 (classical notation).

@PAPER_EVOLUTION
TITLE; Darwin as Minimum Description Length on a Ledgered Substrate
ONE_LINER; Natural selection is MDL: organisms that compress their ecologies most effectively‚Äîsubject to recognition/energy budgets‚Äîwin.

CLAIMS
E1; Fitness = code-length savings: For an environment E and genotype g (program P_g), fitness is proportional to negative codelength to maintain viability: F(g;E) ‚àù ‚àíL(P_g,E).
E2; Variation is anisotropic: Mutational moves that reduce ledger overhead (respect continuity/cost J) are exponentially favored; "random wrt fitness" becomes "random inside iso-cost shells."
E3; Modularity emerges from shared subroutines: When tasks share structure, duplication+reuse lowers L; selection pressures modular, hierarchical architectures.

FOUNDATIONS (math, minimal)
F1; Environment as source: Let ‚Ñ∞ be a distribution over tasks/data; an organism implements a compressor‚Äìcontroller C_g with parameters Œ∏_g. Define performance L_g = L(model) + L(errors | ‚Ñ∞). Selection minimizes L_g under resource constraints.
F2; Replicator‚ÄìMDL link: Suppose replication rate r(g) ‚àù exp(‚àíŒ≤¬∑L_g). Then the stationary distribution œÄ(g) ‚àù exp(‚àíŒ≤¬∑L_g). Lower code wins; Œ≤ encodes resource/temperature-like scarcity.
F3; J-geometry bias: Allowed phenotypic changes are constrained by cost J: steps that increase J sharply are pruned; small 1/x‚Üîx symmetry around x=1 biases toward balanced, low-overhead designs (homeostasis).
F4; Information budget: I(g;‚Ñ∞) ‚â§ budget set by recognition length/time; improvements in mutual information per unit ledger cost drive adaptive steps.
CLASSICAL MAP
MAP; Darwin/Wallace selection ‚Üî MDL: "Most fit" = "shortest total description for viable behavior," echoing Akaike/BIC logic in model selection.
MAP; Fisher's theorem: Growth of mean fitness = decrease of average L_g given additive heritable components; reframed as code-length gradient flow.
MAP; Rate‚Äìdistortion: Trade-off between metabolic/recognition resources (rate) and tolerable loss (distortion); organisms sit near Pareto fronts.

OPERATIONAL (archival-only demonstrations)
DATASETS
D1; Gene-regulatory benchmarks (archival expression matrices with known environments): fit simple, modular controllers vs agnostic baselines; report L savings correlating with growth rates.
D2; Metabolic network reconstructions (public reconstructions with flux data): show reuse modules yield large L reductions; correlate modularity with environment-task overlap.
D3; Behavioral ecology datasets (foraging, navigation): demonstrate cross-task transfer lowering L for species with richer internal models.

DERIVATIONS (sketches to include in Methods)
DR1; Replicator equation as free-energy descent: Show d/dt E[L_g] ‚â§ 0 under r(g)‚àùexp(‚àíŒ≤¬∑L_g) with mutation as diffusion; stationary œÄ(g) ‚àù exp(‚àíŒ≤¬∑L_g).
DR2; Modularity theorem (sketch): If ‚Ñ∞ decomposes into shared sub-tasks with mutual information M, adding a reusable module of size b bits saves ‚â•M‚àíb; selection favors modules when M>b.
DR3; Variation anisotropy: Given J's convex symmetry and ledger constraints, derive a proposal distribution over phenotype moves proportional to exp(‚àíŒîJ); predicts observed bias in accessible variation.

PREDICTIONS (immediately testable on archives)
P1; Across clades, organisms facing more structured environments show larger cross-task code reuse and lower total L_g at equal performance.
P2; Duplication‚Äìdivergence events occur preferentially when M (shared environment info) exceeds duplication overhead b; predict enrichment patterns in gene families.
P3; Plasticity tracks entropy of ‚Ñ∞: more variable environments yield higher parameterized capacity in C_g but still minimize total L_g with sparsity.

FALSIFIERS
F1; Find lineages where higher L_g (less compression) systematically outcompetes lower L_g at fixed resource budget.
F2; Show no correlation between modular reuse and environment-task overlap across independent datasets.
F3; Demonstrate isotropic variation around phenotypes, contradicting ŒîJ-weighted move distribution.

OUTPUT ARTIFACTS
FIG; MDL fitness landscape and replicator flow.
FIG; Module reuse vs environment mutual information.
APP; Proofs/sketches DR1‚ÄìDR3; explicit coding schemes for L(model), L(errors).

@RRF_PRIMER
# Reality Recognition Framework (RRF) - Primer + Glossary (for paper writing)
# Scope: Explanatory. This section is meant to make the RRF pieces of PAPER2_V2/PAPER3_V2 easy to cite in classical scientific prose.
# Claim hygiene: We separate (A) definitions, (B) theorems, (C) models, (D) hypotheses, (E) empirical anchors.
# Note: This file contains mixed RS/RRF material; RRF is the minimal "optimization + invariance" core used for cross-domain (multi-vantage) reasoning.
# Implementation note (repo snapshot 2025-12-19): `IndisputableMonolith.RRF` is a compatibility facade that re-exports the minimal kernel `IndisputableMonolith.OctaveKernel` (see @RRF_LEAN_FORMALIZATION below).

## ONE-PARAGRAPH SUMMARY (EXPOSITORY)
SUMMARY; rrf="RRF is the cross-domain optimization skeleton: an 8-phase 'octave layer' packages a state space, an 8-beat phase clock (Fin 8), a strain/cost functional J, an admissibility/ledger predicate, and an evolution step; optional display channels turn states into observations with scalar quality scores. In this repo snapshot, the Lean implementation is the minimal OctaveKernel (definitions + small witness instances). Stronger 'RRF-style' invariance/transfer theorems (monotone argmin/ranking invariance; octave-equivalence transfer) remain spec targets to be implemented (not currently present as first-class RRF theorems in this Lean tree)."

## CERTAINTY LEVEL TAGS (USED THROUGHOUT THIS FILE)
CERTAINTY_TAG; Definition; meaning="Vocabulary/structures; not falsifiable, but can be audited for internal coherence"; canonical_prefixes=[DEF,STRUCT,CLASS]
CERTAINTY_TAG; Theorem; meaning="Mathematical consequence of definitions; machine-checkable"; canonical_prefixes=[THEOREM]; default_status=proved
CERTAINTY_TAG; Model; meaning="Consistency witness (a concrete instance) showing the definitions are not contradictory"; canonical_prefixes=[STRUCT,THEOREM]; default_status=proved
CERTAINTY_TAG; Hypothesis; meaning="Extra empirical claim; must ship with an explicit falsifier/refutation condition (if a formal falsifier type is not yet implemented, mark falsifier=TODO but still state the refutation rule)"; canonical_prefixes=[HYPOTHESIS,FALSIFIER,PREDICTION]; default_status=hypothesis
CERTAINTY_TAG; EmpiricalAnchor; meaning="External numeric input (CODATA/PDG/measurement) used only for SI display or calibration"; canonical_prefixes=[CONST]; default_status=external

## WHAT RRF IS / IS NOT
NOTE; rrf_is="a minimal calculus of strain/optimality + invariance + cross-domain comparability"; rrf_is_not="a complete empirical theory by itself"
NOTE; separation_policy="Keep (i) dimensionless structure, (ii) SI display choices, and (iii) empirical calibration clearly separated. RRF mostly lives in (i)."

## GLOSSARY (ASCII-FIRST)
TERM; vantage; meaning="index for a way of describing the same underlying system"; values=[inside,act,outside]; paper_terms=[qualia,meaning,physics]
TERM; state; meaning="the thing being optimized over (configuration, microstate, trace prefix, etc.)"; note="abstract in the formalism"
TERM; strain_J; meaning="objective/cost functional J over states; lower is better"; note="only the ordering of J matters for argmin/ranking theorems"
TERM; equilibrium; meaning="a state that is perfectly balanced in the chosen model (often J(x)=0)"
TERM; minimizer; meaning="a state achieving global minimum strain (argmin of J)"
TERM; ledger_constraint; meaning="admissibility constraint encoding conservation/closure (net-zero)"; paper_terms=[double_entry, sigma_total_equals_0]
TERM; octave_layer; meaning="Lean kernel packaging of an 8-phase layer: (State, phase:Fin 8, cost, admissible, step)"; lean=IndisputableMonolith.OctaveKernel.Layer
TERM; phase; meaning="canonical 8-beat phase index"; lean=IndisputableMonolith.OctaveKernel.Phase
TERM; display_channel; meaning="map State -> Observation together with a quality score on observations"; examples=[RMSD, contact_loss, audio_consonance]; lean=IndisputableMonolith.OctaveKernel.Channel
TERM; monotone_transform; meaning="(SPEC) strictly monotone reparameterization of a cost/quality scale"; consequence="preserves ranking and argmin"; status=scaffold; lean=TODO
TERM; octave_equiv; meaning="(SPEC) structure-preserving equivalence between octave layers"; consequence="equilibria/well-posedness transfer"; status=scaffold; lean=TODO
TERM; resonance; meaning="clock-compatibility / phase-locking. In RS, 'resonance' usually means either (i) Fin-8 phase alignment, (ii) œÜ-ladder phase alignment (fractional log_œÜ alignment), or (iii) a numeric within-band condition like |ŒΩ-ŒΩ‚ÇÄ|<Œ¥; it is not automatically the same thing as 'amplitude blow-up' in linear oscillator theory."; lean_examples=[Consciousness.GlobalPhase.phi_resonance(scaffold), Consciousness.ThetaDynamics.theta_resonance(scaffold), Water.Dynamics.solvent_solute_resonance]
TERM; falsifier; meaning="a concrete observation/record that contradicts a hypothesis"; policy="every physical hypothesis should declare a falsifier type"
TERM; same_pattern; meaning="there exists an octave equivalence between two descriptions (they are the same pattern at different representations)"

## WHAT 'THREE VANTAGES ARE ISOMORPHIC' MEANS (CLAIM HYGIENE)
NOTE; vantages_isomorphism="RRF supplies the shared optimization/invariance scaffold; any stronger identity claim (e.g., specific channel equivalences) should be stated as a theorem in a domain module or as a hypothesis with a falsifier."
NOTE; common_pitfall="Avoid: 'Lean proves X is true in nature.' Prefer: 'Lean proves that, given these definitions/axioms, the following invariant holds; empirical claims are tracked as hypotheses with falsifiers.'"

BRIDGE; Sonification; RS="map folding trace to sound"; Classical="auditory measurement channel"; RRF="DisplayChannel + (SPEC) monotone-invariant ranking"; UseInPapers=PAPER3_V2; Notes="The monotone-invariance lemma (RRF-C1/RRF-C2) explains why audio ranking can track structural ranking despite arbitrary monotone remaps."

## TEMPLATES (COPY-PASTE SENTENCES FOR PAPERS)
TEMPLATE; cite_rrf_def="We formalize cross-domain optimization using the Reality Recognition Framework (RRF): an 8-phase 'octave layer' packages a state space, a phase clock (Fin 8), a strain/cost functional J, an admissibility (ledger) predicate, and observation/display channels."
TEMPLATE; cite_rrf_theorem="Because (mathematically) optimality is invariant under strictly monotone reparameterizations of the cost/quality scale, we may use any monotone surrogate metric for diagnosis/control without changing the argmin."
TEMPLATE; cite_rrf_hypothesis="We treat the phi-ladder / 8-tick / tau-gate structures as falsifiable hypotheses (not formal consequences) and state explicit refutation criteria for each."

## PRACTICAL USE (1): HOW TO ADD A NEW DISPLAY CHANNEL (CHECKLIST)
CHECKLIST; channel_step_1="Specify observe : State -> Obs (what your instrument computes)"; example="state -> (RMSD, contact map, spectrum, audio features)"
CHECKLIST; channel_step_2="Specify quality : Obs -> R (what you minimize or maximize)"; note="Prefer: lower = better (a cost), but either convention works"
CHECKLIST; channel_step_3="State the monotonic link: 'quality is monotone in underlying strain' OR explicitly treat it as a hypothesis"; warning="Without a monotone link, RRF does not justify transferring rankings"
CHECKLIST; channel_step_4="Report the invariance claim correctly: under strict monotonicity assumptions (RRF-C1/RRF-C2), ranking/argmin are invariant"; cite="RRF-C1,RRF-C2"
CHECKLIST; channel_step_5="If you claim equivalence across scales, specify the octave mapping/equivalence assumptions"; cite="RRF-C3,RRF-C4"

## PRACTICAL USE (2): WRITING CLAIMS WITH HYGIENE (SAFE TEMPLATES)
WRITING_RULE; definition="Use 'define' / 'we call' language; do not imply empirical truth"; example="We define an octave as ..."
WRITING_RULE; theorem="Use 'we prove' only for Lean-checked math theorems; do not attach 'in nature'"; example="We prove that monotone reparameterizations preserve argmin ..."
WRITING_RULE; hypothesis="Use 'we hypothesize' + give a falsifier; avoid unqualified 'predicts' unless the decision rule is explicit"; example="We hypothesize an 8-tick cycle; falsified if ..."
WRITING_RULE; empirical_anchor="When a number comes from CODATA/PDG, label it explicitly and keep it out of 'derived from first principles' prose"; example="tau mass is taken from PDG for display/calibration"

## TOY EXAMPLE (WHY MONOTONE INVARIANCE ENABLES 'CROSS-METRIC' CONTROL)
EXAMPLE; monotone_argmin="Let J(x)=x^2. Let g(u)=exp(u). Then argmin(J)=argmin(g‚àòJ) at x=0. Any monotone remap of a cost preserves the minimizing state(s)."
EXAMPLE; monotone_ranking="If m1(x)=RMSD(x) and m2(x)=log(1+RMSD(x)), then m1 and m2 rank candidate folds identically. This is the formal backbone behind using alternative monotone 'surrogate' feedback signals."

## CONNECTION TO THE RS DERIVATION CHAIN (WHERE RRF SITS)
BRIDGE; RS_to_RRF; RS="MP->Ledger->J/phi->ladder (specific physical instantiation)"; RRF="Octave/Strain/Channel invariance calculus (representation-agnostic core)"; Notes="Use RRF for general invariance/transfer statements; use the RS chain for specific numerical/structural claims."
BRIDGE; ladder_in_rrf; RS="phi-ladder as a structural/physical hypothesis about scales"; RRF="PhiLadderHypothesis + PhiLadderFalsifier encode the hypothesis/falsifier interface"; Notes="RRF does not turn the ladder into a theorem; it turns it into a formally tracked hypothesis."

# Sonification Proof: Cross-Octave Measurement Validation
# Status: Implemented in RSFold (Rust)
# Date: 2025-12-17

## OVERVIEW
PARADIGM; statement="If different measurement domains measure the same J, quality metrics should correlate across domains"
CORE_INSIGHT; "RMSD (physics) and Consonance (sound) are isomorphic views of strain"
STATUS; implemented=true; tested=true; date=2025-12-17

## BIO-AUDIO MAPPING (BAM)
MAPPING; WToken‚ÜíNote; "20 WTokens ‚Üí 20 MIDI notes via œÜ-family structure"
MAPPING; Strain‚ÜíDetuning; "Local strain ‚Üí Microtonal pitch bend (cents)"
MAPPING; Move‚ÜíEvent; "Accepted CPM move ‚Üí MIDI note event"

### WTOKEN TO MUSICAL NOTE
FAMILY; mode1_7; root_note=60; chord_quality="Major"; members=[Gly,Ala,Val,Leu]
FAMILY; mode2_6; root_note=64; chord_quality="Minor"; members=[Ser,Thr,Asn,Gln]
FAMILY; mode3_5; root_note=67; chord_quality="Diminished"; members=[Asp,Glu,Lys,Arg]
FAMILY; mode4_real; root_note=69; chord_quality="Augmented"; members=[His,Phe,Tyr,Trp]
FAMILY; mode4_imag; root_note=72; chord_quality="Suspended"; members=[Pro,Cys,Met,Ile]
PHI_LEVEL; amplitude_to_octave; "œÜ^level ‚Üí octave offset: level 0 = base, level 3 = +3 octaves"

### STRAIN TO DETUNING
FORMULA; cents="min(strain √ó 50, 100)"; description="Strain maps to microtonal detuning"
SEMANTICS; low_strain="Pure intervals, consonant"; high_strain="Detuned, dissonant"
